# Spelling Bee Word Bank 5x Expansion, Ages 6 to 10

This Markdown file expands the earlier spelling bee word bank to five times the size. It is grouped by age and spelling pattern so it can be reviewed, converted to JSON, and integrated into the spelling bee app.

Important production note: core and curated words are ready for direct use. Auto-screened expansion words are valid dictionary words, but teacher review is recommended before using them in child-facing final lessons, especially for meaning and sentence audio.

Original word count: 719
Expanded 5x word count: 3595

## Count summary

| Age | Recommended grade | Original count | 5x count | Main use in app |
|---:|---|---:|---:|---|
| 6 | Grade 1 | 114 | 570 | sound builder, CVC words, word families |
| 7 | Grade 2 | 153 | 765 | silent e, vowel teams, blends, digraphs |
| 8 | Grade 3 | 134 | 670 | syllables, compounds, suffixes, soft c/g |
| 9 | Grade 4 | 140 | 700 | prefixes, suffixes, silent letters, tricky patterns |
| 10 | Grade 5 | 178 | 890 | advanced spelling bee challenge and morphology |

## Recommended app fields

| Field | Meaning |
|---|---|
| id | Stable app ID for the word |
| word | Spelling word |
| age | Target age level |
| difficulty | easy, medium, hard, or challenge |
| pattern | Main spelling pattern to teach |
| syllableCountHint | Approximate syllable count for sorting |
| gameModes | Suggested games for the word |
| dataTier | core_curated, expanded_curated, or expanded_auto_screened |
| reviewStatus | ready or teacher_review_recommended |

## Full word bank

## Age 6 word bank, 570 words

### ck after short vowel (5 words)

- back, duck, neck, rock, sock

### digraphs sh ch th wh (14 words)

- bath, chin, chip, fish, much, path, rich, ship, shop, that
- thin, this, when, whip

### double consonant endings (4 words)

- buzz, miss, off, well

### short a CVC (23 words)

- bag, bat, can, cat, dad, fan, ham, hat, jam, mad
- man, mat, pad, pan, rag, ram, ran, rat, sad, sat
- tag, van, wag

### short e CVC (12 words)

- bed, fed, hen, jet, led, men, net, pen, pet, red
- ten, wet

### short i CVC (13 words)

- big, bit, dig, fig, fin, hit, kit, pig, pin, sit
- tin, wig, win

### short o CVC (9 words)

- box, dog, fog, fox, hop, log, mop, pop, top

### short u CVC (15 words)

- bud, bug, bun, bus, cup, cut, fun, hug, hut, mud
- nut, pup, rug, run, sun

### simple blends (19 words)

- clap, drop, fast, flag, frog, glad, grip, hand, jump, lamp
- lost, milk, nest, plan, plum, pond, skip, stop, swim

### digraphs and special letter teams (31 words)

- brick, brush, buck, bush, chant, chart, chest, chick, child, clock
- deck, dish, flash, fresh, lock, mouth, quick, shade, shell, shoe
- short, stick, thing, truck, wash, watch, whale, wish, bash, beck
- bock

### general spelling practice (1 words)

- ground

### multisyllable words (6 words)

- lemon, open, seven, under, visit, bale

## Integration notes

1. Use Age 6 and 7 words mainly for Sound to Spelling Builder, Word Family Builder, Missing Letter Detective, and Real Spelling Bee Challenge.
2. Use Age 8 words for syllable splitting, compound words, suffix rules, soft c/g, and longer spelling patterns.
3. Use Age 9 words for prefix and suffix teaching, silent-letter practice, tricky vowel patterns, and academic vocabulary.
4. Use Age 10 words for full spelling bee mode with repeat word, meaning, sentence, syllable hint, first-letter hint, and word-origin hint.
5. Add verified meanings and example sentences before release. The current file focuses on word, age, pattern, difficulty, and game routing.
6. For syllable-specific gameplay, manually verify the syllable split before showing syllable boxes to the child.
